</p>

<p>The <b>2013 Malaysian Grand Prix</b> (officially the <b>2013 Formula 1 Petronas Malaysia Grand Prix</b>) was a Formula One motor race held at the <a href="/wiki/Sepang_International_Circuit" title="Sepang International Circuit">Sepang International Circuit</a> in <a href="/wiki/Sepang_(town)" title="Sepang (town)">Sepang</a>, <a href="/wiki/Selangor" title="Selangor">Selangor</a> on 24 March 2013 before 90,000 people. It was the second round of the <a href="/wiki/2013_Formula_One_World_Championship" title="2013 Formula One World Championship">2013 Formula One World Championship</a>, and the 15th Formula One Malaysian race. <a href="/wiki/Red_Bull_Racing" title="Red Bull Racing">Red Bull</a> driver <a href="/wiki/Sebastian_Vettel" title="Sebastian Vettel">Sebastian Vettel</a> won the 56-lap race from <a href="/wiki/Pole_position" title="Pole position">pole position</a>. His teammate <a href="/wiki/Mark_Webber" title="Mark Webber">Mark Webber</a> finished second, and <a href="/wiki/Lewis_Hamilton" title="Lewis Hamilton">Lewis Hamilton</a> was third for the <a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_in_Formula_One" title="Mercedes-Benz in Formula One">Mercedes</a> team.
</p><p>The race began on a damp track after an earlier downpour, with Vettel in pole position alongside <a href="/wiki/Felipe_Massa" title="Felipe Massa">Felipe Massa</a> of <a href="/wiki/Scuderia_Ferrari" title="Scuderia Ferrari">Ferrari</a>; Massa's teammate <a href="/wiki/Fernando_Alonso" title="Fernando Alonso">Fernando Alonso</a>, and Hamilton began from third and fourth. Webber moved from fifth to second by the second lap, and took the lead after Vettel made his first <a href="/wiki/Pit_stop" title="Pit stop">pit stop</a> for dry slick tyres on lap five. He maintained that position through most of the race until Vettel ignored a <a href="/wiki/Team_orders" title="Team orders">team order</a> from Red Bull to lower the performance of his engine, overtaking Webber for the lead on the 46th lap. Vettel maintained the lead for the final nine laps for his first victory of the season, his third in Malaysia, and the 27th of his career. Hamilton finished 12&#160;seconds behind, and his teammate <a href="/wiki/Nico_Rosberg" title="Nico Rosberg">Nico Rosberg</a> was told by Mercedes team principal <a href="/wiki/Ross_Brawn" title="Ross Brawn">Ross Brawn</a> to hold fourth place.
</p><p>Vettel apologised to the Red Bull team and Webber for ignoring the order to hold position; Red Bull did not punish or reprimand him because his attorneys threatened legal action, and he recanted the apology three weeks later. Webber was asked to present his version of events to Red Bull founder and co-owner <a href="/wiki/Dietrich_Mateschitz" title="Dietrich Mateschitz">Dietrich Mateschitz</a>. Vettel's victory placed him in the lead of the <a href="/wiki/List_of_Formula_One_World_Drivers%27_Champions" title="List of Formula One World Drivers&#39; Champions">World Drivers' Championship</a>, after <a href="/wiki/Lotus_F1" title="Lotus F1">Lotus</a> driver <a href="/wiki/Kimi_R%C3%A4ikk%C3%B6nen" title="Kimi Räikkönen">Kimi Räikkönen</a> finished seventh. Webber and Hamilton moved from third to fourth position. Red Bull took the lead of the <a href="/wiki/List_of_Formula_One_World_Constructors%27_Champions" title="List of Formula One World Constructors&#39; Champions">World Constructors' Championship</a> from Ferrari, with seventeen races left in the season.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Background">Background</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2013_Malaysian_Grand_Prix&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Background">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Bird-eye_view_of_Sepang_F1_Circuit_-_panoramio.jpg" class="image"><img alt="Aerial photo of the track" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c9/Bird-eye_view_of_Sepang_F1_Circuit_-_panoramio.jpg/220px-Bird-eye_view_of_Sepang_F1_Circuit_-_panoramio.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="165" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c9/Bird-eye_view_of_Sepang_F1_Circuit_-_panoramio.jpg/330px-Bird-eye_view_of_Sepang_F1_Circuit_-_panoramio.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c9/Bird-eye_view_of_Sepang_F1_Circuit_-_panoramio.jpg/440px-Bird-eye_view_of_Sepang_F1_Circuit_-_panoramio.jpg 2x" data-file-width="5152" data-file-height="3864" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Bird-eye_view_of_Sepang_F1_Circuit_-_panoramio.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>The <a href="/wiki/Sepang_International_Circuit" title="Sepang International Circuit">Sepang International Circuit</a> <i>(pictured in 2016)</i>, where the race was held</div></div></div>
<p>The 2013 <a href="/wiki/Malaysian_Grand_Prix" title="Malaysian Grand Prix">Malaysian Grand Prix</a> was the 2nd of the 19 rounds of the <a href="/wiki/2013_Formula_One_World_Championship" title="2013 Formula One World Championship">2013 Formula One World Championship</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-CF1Overview_1-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CF1Overview-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup> and the 15th <a href="/wiki/Formula_One" title="Formula One">Formula One</a> Malaysian race.<sup id="cite_ref-BRPreview_3-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BRPreview-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> It was held at the 15-turn 5.543&#160;km (3.444&#160;mi) <a href="/wiki/Sepang_International_Circuit" title="Sepang International Circuit">Sepang International Circuit</a> in <a href="/wiki/Sepang_(town)" title="Sepang (town)">Sepang</a>, <a href="/wiki/Selangor" title="Selangor">Selangor</a> on 24 March.<sup id="cite_ref-RETechReview_4-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-RETechReview-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup> A <a href="/wiki/F%C3%A9d%C3%A9ration_Internationale_de_l%27Automobile" title="Fédération Internationale de l&#39;Automobile">Fédération Internationale de l'Automobile</a> (FIA, motorsport's governing body)-sanctioned race has been held in Malaysia since the 1960s, with the first editions run in <a href="/wiki/Singapore" title="Singapore">Singapore</a>—then part of the Malaysian Federation—before moving to the <a href="/wiki/Shah_Alam_Circuit" title="Shah Alam Circuit">Shah Alam Circuit</a>. With the arrival of Formula One in <a href="/wiki/1999_Malaysian_Grand_Prix" title="1999 Malaysian Grand Prix">1999</a>, the race was moved to the purpose-built Sepang International Circuit, where all editions were held until <a href="/wiki/2017_Malaysian_Grand_Prix" title="2017 Malaysian Grand Prix">2017</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p><a href="/wiki/Formula_One_tyres" title="Formula One tyres">Tyre</a> supplier <a href="/wiki/Pirelli" title="Pirelli">Pirelli</a> brought white-banded, medium compound tyres; red-banded, hard compound dry tyres; green-banded, intermediate compound tyres; and dark-blue-banded <a href="/wiki/Rain_tyre" title="Rain tyre">wet-weather tyres</a> to the race.<sup id="cite_ref-F1RacingMag_2-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-F1RacingMag-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup> The <a href="/wiki/Drag_reduction_system" title="Drag reduction system">drag reduction system</a> (DRS), an adjustable flap at the back of each car that helps with overtaking when activated, had two activation zones for the race: one on the <a href="/wiki/Straight_(racing)" title="Straight (racing)">straight</a>, linking turns 14 and 15, and another on the straight between the final and first corners.<sup id="cite_ref-BRPreview_3-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BRPreview-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> For the race, a debris fence on the <a href="/wiki/Pit_stop" title="Pit stop">pit lane</a> wall was extended to better safeguard <a href="/wiki/Motorsport_marshal" title="Motorsport marshal">track marshals</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-RETechReview_4-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-RETechReview-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After winning the season-opening <a href="/wiki/2013_Australian_Grand_Prix" title="2013 Australian Grand Prix">Australian Grand Prix</a> one week earlier, <a href="/wiki/Lotus_F1" title="Lotus F1">Lotus</a> driver <a href="/wiki/Kimi_R%C3%A4ikk%C3%B6nen" title="Kimi Räikkönen">Kimi Räikkönen</a> led the <a href="/wiki/List_of_Formula_One_World_Drivers%27_Champions" title="List of Formula One World Drivers&#39; Champions">World Drivers' Championship</a> with 25 <a href="/wiki/List_of_Formula_One_World_Championship_points_scoring_systems" title="List of Formula One World Championship points scoring systems">points</a>, ahead of <a href="/wiki/Scuderia_Ferrari" title="Scuderia Ferrari">Ferrari</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Fernando_Alonso" title="Fernando Alonso">Fernando Alonso</a> and <a href="/wiki/Red_Bull_Racing" title="Red Bull Racing">Red Bull</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Sebastian_Vettel" title="Sebastian Vettel">Sebastian Vettel</a> in second and third, with 18 and 15 points. Alonso's teammate <a href="/wiki/Felipe_Massa" title="Felipe Massa">Felipe Massa</a> was fourth with 12 points, and <a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_in_Formula_One" title="Mercedes-Benz in Formula One">Mercedes</a> driver <a href="/wiki/Lewis_Hamilton" title="Lewis Hamilton">Lewis Hamilton</a> was fifth with ten points.<sup id="cite_ref-2013Points_6-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2013Points-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup> Ferrari led the <a href="/wiki/List_of_Formula_One_World_Constructors%27_Champions" title="List of Formula One World Constructors&#39; Champions">World Constructors' Championship</a> with 30 points; Lotus and Ferrari followed with 26 and 23 points, respectively. Mercedes and <a href="/wiki/Force_India" title="Force India">Force India</a> held fourth place, with ten points each.<sup id="cite_ref-2013Points_6-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2013Points-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Vettel said that the Australian Grand Prix would be meaningless later in the year, and predicted that with the different conditions and tyres in Malaysia, he would outpace Ferrari and Lotus.<sup id="cite_ref-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> His teammate, <a href="/wiki/Mark_Webber" title="Mark Webber">Mark Webber</a>, explained that Red Bull required an improvement in car performance for the race: "As a team we weren't as strong as we thought we'd be. But that's Formula One – it can change very quickly. We've got a very, very hot track this week in Sepang. So let's see how we go for the next few races. It's the first marker in the sand."<sup id="cite_ref-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup> Hamilton said that Mercedes would bring what they learnt about team strategy from Melbourne to Sepang, and would have good results if his team then scored ten points.<sup id="cite_ref-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>For the second consecutive race, reliability issues with the telemetry link between race control and the cars prompted the FIA to disable the system, stopping teams from informing drivers of an incident or being lapped, and the FIA could not disable DRS in inclement weather or a <a href="/wiki/Safety_car" title="Safety car">safety car</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-:1_10-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:1-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> The stewards advised drivers to comply with DRS usage rules, and required teams to inform them when the system was disabled.<sup id="cite_ref-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> If officials deployed the safety car, drivers were ordered to manually press a button on their <a href="/wiki/Steering_wheel" title="Steering wheel">steering wheel</a> to slow their cars as soon as they noticed a warning board or an illuminated light. Drivers acquainted themselves with the revised procedures in a test held after the third practice session.<sup id="cite_ref-:1_10-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:1-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Nico_Hulkenberg_2013_Malaysia_FP2.jpg" class="image"><img alt="Nico Hulkenberg during a practice session" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/28/Nico_Hulkenberg_2013_Malaysia_FP2.jpg/220px-Nico_Hulkenberg_2013_Malaysia_FP2.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="110" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/28/Nico_Hulkenberg_2013_Malaysia_FP2.jpg/330px-Nico_Hulkenberg_2013_Malaysia_FP2.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/28/Nico_Hulkenberg_2013_Malaysia_FP2.jpg/440px-Nico_Hulkenberg_2013_Malaysia_FP2.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2560" data-file-height="1280" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Nico_Hulkenberg_2013_Malaysia_FP2.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Nico Hülkenberg was given a new C32 chassis by the Sauber team.</div></div></div>
<p>Several teams made changes to their cars for the race.<sup id="cite_ref-RETechReview_4-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-RETechReview-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Sauber_Motorsport" title="Sauber Motorsport">Sauber</a> introduced a new <a href="/wiki/Sauber_C32" title="Sauber C32">C32</a> chassis for driver <a href="/wiki/Nico_H%C3%BClkenberg" title="Nico Hülkenberg">Nico Hülkenberg</a> after a fuel-system fault prevented him from starting the Australian Grand Prix.<sup id="cite_ref-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> Sauber modified the C32's engine cover to remove hot air from its engine and <a href="/wiki/Glossary_of_motorsport_terms#S" title="Glossary of motorsport terms">sidepods</a>, and added a small vertical fin to improve airflow to the car's rear and <a href="/wiki/Diffuser_(automotive)" title="Diffuser (automotive)">diffuser</a>'s side channels.<sup id="cite_ref-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup> Red Bull installed extra cooling outlets on the centre of the <a href="/wiki/Red_Bull_RB9" title="Red Bull RB9">RB9</a>, to counter Malaysia's warm climate.<sup id="cite_ref-RETechReview_4-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-RETechReview-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup> Ferrari opened the exhausts on the <a href="/wiki/Ferrari_F138" title="Ferrari F138">F138</a> to improve the extraction of warm air from its sidepods.<sup id="cite_ref-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup> Mercedes changed the <a href="/wiki/Bargeboard_(aerodynamics)" title="Bargeboard (aerodynamics)">turning vanes</a> and pillars under the <a href="/wiki/Mercedes_F1_W04" title="Mercedes F1 W04">F1 W04</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> Lotus introduced a new <a href="/wiki/Exhaust_system" title="Exhaust system">exhaust system</a> on Räikkönen's <a href="/wiki/Lotus_E21" title="Lotus E21">E21</a> car and its endplate, main plane and revised upper flap,<sup id="cite_ref-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup> in addition to a revised diffuser with a <a href="/wiki/Gurney_flap" title="Gurney flap">gurney flap</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-RETechReview_4-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-RETechReview-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Practice">Practice</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2013_Malaysian_Grand_Prix&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Practice">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Kimi_Raikkonen_2013_Malaysia_FP1.jpg" class="image"><img alt="Kimi Räikkönen in a practice session" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d3/Kimi_Raikkonen_2013_Malaysia_FP1.jpg/220px-Kimi_Raikkonen_2013_Malaysia_FP1.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="110" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d3/Kimi_Raikkonen_2013_Malaysia_FP1.jpg/330px-Kimi_Raikkonen_2013_Malaysia_FP1.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d3/Kimi_Raikkonen_2013_Malaysia_FP1.jpg/440px-Kimi_Raikkonen_2013_Malaysia_FP1.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2560" data-file-height="1281" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Kimi_Raikkonen_2013_Malaysia_FP1.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>During the first practice session, <a href="/wiki/Kimi_R%C3%A4ikk%C3%B6nen" title="Kimi Räikkönen">Kimi Räikkönen</a> was restricted due to a <a href="/wiki/Kinetic_energy_recovery_system" title="Kinetic energy recovery system">kinetic energy recovery system</a> battery change.</div></div></div>
<p>In accordance with the 2013 regulations, three practice sessions were held: two 90-minute sessions on Friday, and another 60-minute session on Saturday.<sup id="cite_ref-2013Regs_17-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2013Regs-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup> The first practice session was held in hot, humid weather; no driver set a competitive lap time for 34 minutes. Several drivers remained in the <a href="/wiki/Pit_stop" title="Pit stop">pit lane</a> to wait for better track conditions to record their quickest times in a ten-minute period of successive laps, before running a heavy fuel load.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportFP1_18-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportFP1-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup> Webber's first timed lap (1 minute, 37.588 seconds) was followed by 1 minute, 37.354 seconds from his teammate Vettel. Webber improved to a 1-minute, 36.395-second lap to go fastest.<sup id="cite_ref-BBCSport_19-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCSport-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup> Räikkönen, who missed the first 55 minutes as Lotus replaced a <a href="/wiki/Kinetic_energy_recovery_system" title="Kinetic energy recovery system">kinetic energy recovery system</a> (KERS) battery which failed due to a sensor problem,<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportFP1_18-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportFP1-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup> was the second-fastest.<sup id="cite_ref-BBCSport_19-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCSport-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup> Vettel, Alonso, <a href="/wiki/Nico_Rosberg" title="Nico Rosberg">Nico Rosberg</a> of Mercedes, <a href="/wiki/Adrian_Sutil" title="Adrian Sutil">Adrian Sutil</a> of Force India, Massa, <a href="/wiki/Paul_di_Resta" title="Paul di Resta">Paul di Resta</a>, Hamilton and Lotus driver <a href="/wiki/Romain_Grosjean" title="Romain Grosjean">Romain Grosjean</a> were second to tenth.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportFP1_18-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportFP1-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup> Sutil damaged his front wing on a <a href="/wiki/Curb" title="Curb">kerb</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportFP1_18-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportFP1-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup> and Sauber's <a href="/wiki/Esteban_Guti%C3%A9rrez" title="Esteban Gutiérrez">Esteban Gutiérrez</a> spun at turn 14.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportRaceHughes_21-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportRaceHughes-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>The second session was also hot and humid;<sup id="cite_ref-BBCFP2_22-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCFP2-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup> many teams used dry tyres early, due to rain clouds above the track. A heavy rain shower fell, preventing an improvement in lap times; some drivers drove on the wet track on the intermediate-compound tyres, to acclimatise themselves with the conditions if inclement weather returned later in the week.<sup id="cite_ref-NBCFP2_23-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-NBCFP2-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup> Räikkönen lapped fastest at 1 minute, 36.569 seconds, followed by Vettel, Massa and Alonso, Webber, Grosjean, Rosberg, Di Resta, Hamilton and Sutil.<sup id="cite_ref-BBCFP2_22-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCFP2-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup> Some drivers went off the track during the session, due to wetness.<sup id="cite_ref-NBCFP2_23-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-NBCFP2-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-ESPNFP2_25-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ESPNFP2-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup> Gutiérrez's in-car <a href="/wiki/Fire_extinguisher" title="Fire extinguisher">fire extinguisher</a> activated after mounting the turn-12 kerb, and a subsequent exhaust-system fracture ended his session.<sup id="cite_ref-ESPNFP2_25-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ESPNFP2-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In the final session (also in hot, humid weather), most drivers used hard-compound tyres to see how they would behave during the race, then switched to medium-compound tyres when track <a href="/wiki/Grip_(auto_racing)" title="Grip (auto racing)">grip</a> improved.<sup id="cite_ref-26" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup> Räikkönen set a benchmark in the first ten minutes, which Rosberg and Sutil bettered. Rosberg and his teammate, Hamilton, fought for the fastest lap time until Vettel used the medium-compound tyres to lead with a 1 minute, 36.435-second lap with three minutes to go. Hamilton, Sutil, Webber, Räikkönen, Di Resta, McLaren's <a href="/wiki/Jenson_Button" title="Jenson Button">Jenson Button</a>, Massa, Rosberg and Alonso were the ten fastest drivers.<sup id="cite_ref-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup> Near the end of the session, Hamilton's right-front tyre tore a tread<sup id="cite_ref-28" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup> after he locked the wheel and <a href="/wiki/Flat_spot" title="Flat spot">flat-spotted</a> it to the canvas.<sup id="cite_ref-ESPNFP3_29-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ESPNFP3-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup> Part of the tyre detached on the backstraight, and damaged Hamilton's front wing.<sup id="cite_ref-ESPNFP3_29-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ESPNFP3-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Qualifying">Qualifying</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2013_Malaysian_Grand_Prix&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Qualifying">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Sebastian_Vettel_2013_Malaysia_FP2.jpg" class="image"><img alt="Sebastian Vettel during the second practice session" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a9/Sebastian_Vettel_2013_Malaysia_FP2.jpg/220px-Sebastian_Vettel_2013_Malaysia_FP2.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="110" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a9/Sebastian_Vettel_2013_Malaysia_FP2.jpg/330px-Sebastian_Vettel_2013_Malaysia_FP2.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a9/Sebastian_Vettel_2013_Malaysia_FP2.jpg/440px-Sebastian_Vettel_2013_Malaysia_FP2.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2560" data-file-height="1280" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Sebastian_Vettel_2013_Malaysia_FP2.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Sebastian_Vettel" title="Sebastian Vettel">Sebastian Vettel</a> took his second pole position of the season and the 38th of his career.</div></div></div>
<p>Saturday afternoon's <a href="/wiki/Glossary_of_motorsport_terms#Q" title="Glossary of motorsport terms">qualifying session</a> was divided into three parts. The first session lasted 18 minutes, eliminating cars which finished the session 17th or below. The <a href="/wiki/107%25_rule" title="107% rule">107% rule</a> was in effect, requiring drivers to reach a time within 107 per cent of the fastest lap to qualify. The second session lasted 15 minutes, eliminating cars that finished 11th to 16th. The final, ten-minute session determined <a href="/wiki/Pole_position" title="Pole position">pole position</a> to tenth place. Drivers who progressed to the final session were not allowed to change tyres for the race's start, and used the tyres with which they set their fastest lap times.<sup id="cite_ref-2013Regs_17-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2013Regs-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup> A sudden downpour five minutes before the end of the second session<sup id="cite_ref-PAQuali_30-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PAQuali-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup> wet the track from turns five to six, prompting the drivers to switch to intermediate-compound tyres during the session.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportRaceHughes_21-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportRaceHughes-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup> Vettel used a single set of medium-compound tyres in the first and second sessions to prevent tyre overuse.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportRaceHughes_21-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportRaceHughes-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup> He also used intermediate-compound tyres in the final minutes of the third session to take his second pole position of the season and the 38th of his career with a one-minute, 49.674-second lap. Massa started second for the first time since the <a href="/wiki/2010_Bahrain_Grand_Prix" title="2010 Bahrain Grand Prix">2010 Bahrain Grand Prix</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-PAQuali_30-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PAQuali-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup> and was faster than his teammate, Alonso (in third), for the fourth race in a row.<sup id="cite_ref-BBCQuali_31-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCQuali-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup> Hamilton used an older set of intermediate tyres in Mercedes' strategy to remain on the circuit, and qualified fourth. Webber took fifth on one set of intermediate tyres; a pit-wall miscommunication at the end of the final session allowed Hamilton past and stopped him from going faster.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportRaceHughes_21-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportRaceHughes-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup> 
</p>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Felipe_Massa_2013_Malaysia_FP2_2.jpg" class="image"><img alt="Felipe Massa during the second practice session" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1f/Felipe_Massa_2013_Malaysia_FP2_2.jpg/220px-Felipe_Massa_2013_Malaysia_FP2_2.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="110" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1f/Felipe_Massa_2013_Malaysia_FP2_2.jpg/330px-Felipe_Massa_2013_Malaysia_FP2_2.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1f/Felipe_Massa_2013_Malaysia_FP2_2.jpg/440px-Felipe_Massa_2013_Malaysia_FP2_2.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2560" data-file-height="1280" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Felipe_Massa_2013_Malaysia_FP2_2.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Felipe Massa began from second place for the first time since the <a href="/wiki/2010_Bahrain_Grand_Prix" title="2010 Bahrain Grand Prix">2010 Bahrain Grand Prix</a>.</div></div></div>
<p>Rosberg was fastest in the first session,<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportRaceHughes_21-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportRaceHughes-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup> but fell to sixth in the final session on a used set of intermediate tyres.<sup id="cite_ref-QualiQuotes_32-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-QualiQuotes-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup> Räikkönen took seventh on a new set of intermediate tyres.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportRaceHughes_21-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportRaceHughes-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup> A slow pace put Button eighth, an <a href="/wiki/Understeer_and_oversteer" title="Understeer and oversteer">oversteer</a> in the corners left Sutil ninth, and McLaren's <a href="/wiki/Sergio_P%C3%A9rez" title="Sergio Pérez">Sergio Pérez</a> was tenth.<sup id="cite_ref-QualiQuotes_32-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-QualiQuotes-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup> Grosjean, 11th, drove onto the track too late.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportRaceHughes_21-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportRaceHughes-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup> Hülkenberg, 12th, could not switch from a set of worn medium-compound tyres due to a loss of weather data. A car-balance adjustment put <a href="/wiki/Daniel_Ricciardo" title="Daniel Ricciardo">Daniel Ricciardo</a>, of the <a href="/wiki/Scuderia_Toro_Rosso" title="Scuderia Toro Rosso">Toro Rosso</a> team 13th.<sup id="cite_ref-QualiQuotes_32-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-QualiQuotes-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup> The rain caught out Gutiérrez in 14th on dry tyres.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportRaceHughes_21-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportRaceHughes-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup> Di Resta aborted a timed lap due to the rain, prompting Force India to call him to the pit lane for a tyre change.<sup id="cite_ref-BBCQuali_31-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCQuali-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup> He took 15th, rejoining the track when the rain fell and making two errors.<sup id="cite_ref-PAQuali_30-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PAQuali-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Williams_Grand_Prix_Engineering" title="Williams Grand Prix Engineering">Williams</a> driver <a href="/wiki/Pastor_Maldonado" title="Pastor Maldonado">Pastor Maldonado</a>, in 16th, set no lap time; he aborted when the rain began. <a href="/wiki/Jean-%C3%89ric_Vergne" title="Jean-Éric Vergne">Jean-Éric Vergne</a>'s Toro Rosso, 17th, failed to advance beyond the first session after a slower car obstructed him on his lap. Williams' <a href="/wiki/Valtteri_Bottas" title="Valtteri Bottas">Valtteri Bottas</a> recorded the 18th-fastest time, due to poor grip from the medium-compound tyre. The <a href="/wiki/Marussia_F1" title="Marussia F1">Marussia</a> cars of <a href="/wiki/Jules_Bianchi" title="Jules Bianchi">Jules Bianchi</a> and <a href="/wiki/Max_Chilton" title="Max Chilton">Max Chilton</a> were 19th and 21st; they were separated by <a href="/wiki/Charles_Pic" title="Charles Pic">Charles Pic</a>'s Caterham, who had an understeer on his first lap that a pressure adjustment for his second did not remove. <a href="/wiki/Giedo_van_der_Garde" title="Giedo van der Garde">Giedo van der Garde</a>, 22nd, was slowed by an oversteer on the medium-compound tyres.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportRaceHughes_21-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportRaceHughes-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-QualiQuotes_32-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-QualiQuotes-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Post-qualifying">Post-qualifying</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2013_Malaysian_Grand_Prix&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Post-qualifying">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>After qualifying, the stewards imposed a three-place grid penalty on Räikkönen after they concluded that he blocked Rosberg between turns 12 and 15 in the third session. This moved Button to seventh, Sutil to eighth and Pérez to ninth.<sup id="cite_ref-:0_33-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:0-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Qualifying_classification">Qualifying classification</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2013_Malaysian_Grand_Prix&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Qualifying classification">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The fastest lap in each of the three sessions is in <b>bold</b>.

<ul><li><span class="citation wikicite" id="endnote_1"><b><a href="#ref_1">^1</a></b></span> &#160;— <a href="/wiki/Kimi_R%C3%A4ikk%C3%B6nen" title="Kimi Räikkönen">Kimi Räikkönen</a> incurred a three-place grid penalty for blocking <a href="/wiki/Nico_Rosberg" title="Nico Rosberg">Nico Rosberg</a> while qualifying.<sup id="cite_ref-:0_33-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:0-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Race">Race</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2013_Malaysian_Grand_Prix&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Race">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Valtteri_Bottas_2013_Malaysia_FP1.jpg" class="image"><img alt="Valtteri Bottas during the first practice session" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a4/Valtteri_Bottas_2013_Malaysia_FP1.jpg/220px-Valtteri_Bottas_2013_Malaysia_FP1.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="110" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a4/Valtteri_Bottas_2013_Malaysia_FP1.jpg/330px-Valtteri_Bottas_2013_Malaysia_FP1.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a4/Valtteri_Bottas_2013_Malaysia_FP1.jpg/440px-Valtteri_Bottas_2013_Malaysia_FP1.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2560" data-file-height="1280" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Valtteri_Bottas_2013_Malaysia_FP1.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Valtteri_Bottas" title="Valtteri Bottas">Valtteri Bottas</a> began the race with a new front wing after damaging one on a reconnaissance lap in which he aquaplaned into a gravel trap.</div></div></div>
<p>The 56-lap race was held during the afternoon on 24 March.<sup id="cite_ref-CF1Overview_1-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CF1Overview-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup> Thunderstorms were forecast,<sup id="cite_ref-BRPreview_3-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BRPreview-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> and a 30-minute torrential downpour half an hour before the start made the track wet.<sup id="cite_ref-PAALOOut_35-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PAALOOut-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup> The air temperature was 24 to 25&#160;°C (75 to 77&#160;°F), and the track temperature ranged from 27 to 33&#160;°C (81 to 91&#160;°F).<sup id="cite_ref-36" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup> 90,000 people were in attendance.<sup id="cite_ref-37" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Water_stagnation" title="Water stagnation">Standing water</a> caused light spray and impaired visibility, and all cars used intermediate tyres.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportLiveRace_38-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportLiveRace-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup> Turn three was flooded, causing several drivers to <a href="/wiki/Aquaplaning" title="Aquaplaning">aquaplane</a> into a <a href="/wiki/Run-off_area" title="Run-off area">gravel trap</a> before the race. Bottas damaged his front wing; after an assessment, the Williams team repaired it on the grid.<sup id="cite_ref-ESPNRace_39-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ESPNRace-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-BBCWebRace_40-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCWebRace-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup> Williams also changed Maldonado's engine the morning of the event due to <a href="/wiki/Piston" title="Piston">piston</a> damage in qualifying; Maldonado did not incur a penalty because he switched to another of his eight allocated engines for 2013.<sup id="cite_ref-41" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>When the five red lights went out to begin the race,<sup id="cite_ref-ESPNRace_39-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ESPNRace-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup> Vettel maintained his lead into the first corner.<sup id="cite_ref-STRace_42-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-STRace-42">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup> Massa and Alonso veered towards each other behind him, with Hamilton on the left and Webber on the right. Alonso entered turn two in second position, and was surprised by Vettel's perceived early braking. He hit the rear of Vettel's car, which put him wide and damaged his front wing. Webber overtook both Mercedes to move into third place, and battled Alonso for second on the first lap.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportRaceHughes_21-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportRaceHughes-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup> The left front section of Alonso's front wing scraped the tarmac surface;<sup id="cite_ref-SkyF1Race_43-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-SkyF1Race-43">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup> Ferrari kept him on the circuit, anticipating that it would not detach.<sup id="cite_ref-44" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-44">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup> Further down the field, Massa was blocked by other cars and fell from second to sixth.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportLiveRace_38-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportLiveRace-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup> Hülkenberg made a fast start to advance from 12th to ninth, as Pérez moved up from tenth to eighth.<sup id="cite_ref-ESPNRace_39-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ESPNRace-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Fernando_Alonso_Sepang_2013.jpg" class="image"><img alt="Fernando Alonso, off the track" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d9/Fernando_Alonso_Sepang_2013.jpg/220px-Fernando_Alonso_Sepang_2013.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="139" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d9/Fernando_Alonso_Sepang_2013.jpg/330px-Fernando_Alonso_Sepang_2013.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d9/Fernando_Alonso_Sepang_2013.jpg/440px-Fernando_Alonso_Sepang_2013.jpg 2x" data-file-width="980" data-file-height="621" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Fernando_Alonso_Sepang_2013.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Fernando_Alonso" title="Fernando Alonso">Fernando Alonso</a> retired when his front wing became lodged under his Ferrari and prevented him from steering it.</div></div></div>
<p>At the start of lap two, Webber drew alongside Alonso,<sup id="cite_ref-BBCWebRace_40-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCWebRace-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup> whose front wing detached and folded under his Ferrari at the end of the main straight,<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportRaceHughes_21-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportRaceHughes-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup> sending him into the turn-one gravel trap. Track stewards refused Alonso's request to extricate his car from the gravel, and he was the race's first retirement.<sup id="cite_ref-BBCWebRace_40-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCWebRace-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Drag_reduction_system" title="Drag reduction system">DRS</a> was enabled on the third lap.<sup id="cite_ref-STRace_42-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-STRace-42">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup> Rosberg passed Button for fourth on the third lap;<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportLiveRace_38-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportLiveRace-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup> Räikkönen tried to pass Ricciardo for tenth at turn one on the next lap,<sup id="cite_ref-ESPNRace_39-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ESPNRace-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup> but ran wide and dropped to 12th position.<sup id="cite_ref-STRace_42-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-STRace-42">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup> Hülkenberg passed Pérez on the inside for seventh at turn one, and tried unsuccessfully to regain the position on the outside at turn two on lap five.<sup id="cite_ref-ESPNRace_39-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ESPNRace-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup> As lap times fell,<sup id="cite_ref-AutoblogRace_45-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutoblogRace-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup> Vettel made a pit stop from the lead at the end lap four to switch to medium-compound tyres.<sup id="cite_ref-BBCWebRace_40-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCWebRace-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup> He struggled for grip on a damp area, falling behind Pérez, Sutil and Grosjean on lap six,<sup id="cite_ref-BBCWebRace_40-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCWebRace-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup> until he drove onto a dry section and overtook Grosjean; Sutil blocked his attempt to pass at turn 13. On lap seven, Vettel overtook Pérez for seventh place.<sup id="cite_ref-ESPNRace_39-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ESPNRace-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Webber led laps five to seven,<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportRaceHughes_21-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportRaceHughes-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup> because Red Bull advised him that turn three was too wet for dry tyres and he set a series of fast lap times.<sup id="cite_ref-BBCWebRace_40-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCWebRace-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-AutoblogRace_45-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutoblogRace-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup> His <a href="/wiki/Race_engineer" title="Race engineer">race engineer</a>, <a href="/wiki/Simon_Rennie" title="Simon Rennie">Simon Rennie</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-WebberAutoBio_46-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-WebberAutoBio-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup> told him to enter the pit lane on the seventh lap.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportRaceHughes_21-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportRaceHughes-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup> Hamilton made a pit stop on lap eight.<sup id="cite_ref-BBCWebRace_40-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCWebRace-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup> He mistakenly drove into the McLaren pit stall, and the team waved him through to prepare for Button and Pérez's arrival. On that lap, Toro Rosso released Vergne into the path of Pic and they made contact; both drivers had their front wings replaced.<sup id="cite_ref-ESPNRace_39-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ESPNRace-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup> The stewards ruled that Vergne was released unsafely into Pic's path and fined the Toro Rosso team $10,000, but Vergne did not incur a post-race time penalty.<sup id="cite_ref-47" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-47">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup> Rosberg led the eighth lap, until his first stop. After the pit stops, Webber led teammate Vettel and Hamilton. On lap nine, Grosjean passed Ricciardo for ninth position. His teammate, Räikkönen, unsuccessfully attempted to do the same at turn nine. He tried again, and overtook Ricciardo with DRS on the <a href="/wiki/Hairpin_turn" title="Hairpin turn">hairpin turn</a>. Two laps later, Grosjean used DRS to pass Pérez for eighth position.<sup id="cite_ref-ESPNRace_39-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ESPNRace-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup> On the 12th lap, Räikkönen unsuccessfully tried to pass Pérez for ninth into turn one.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportLiveRace_38-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportLiveRace-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Maldonado, in 12th position, ran on a damp white line at turn 11 on lap 13; he drove across the gravel trap, removing half of his car's front wing. Maldonado recovered to the pit lane without external aid for a replacement front wing, and rejoined the race in 21st place.<sup id="cite_ref-ESPNRace_39-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ESPNRace-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-BBCWebRace_40-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCWebRace-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup> By lap 15 Webber led teammate Vettel by 2.2 seconds, and Vettel was the same distance ahead of Hamilton in third.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportLiveRace_38-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportLiveRace-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup> Webber began the second round of pit stops when he entered the pit lane to switch to medium-compound tyres at the end of that lap; he returned to the track in fifth, behind Button.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportLiveRace_38-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportLiveRace-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup> Vettel took the lead and was instructed by his race engineer, Guillaume Rocquelin, to speed up to retain the position. He and Rosberg made their second pit stops at the end of lap 22. Vettel and Rosberg returned to the track in third and fourth place, and Webber returned to the lead.<sup id="cite_ref-BBCWebRace_40-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCWebRace-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup> A recurring captive <a href="/wiki/Lug_nut" title="Lug nut">wheel-nut</a> system fault, possibly caused by a high temperature on the left front wheel, caused Sutil to lose 84 seconds in a pit stop, and dropped him to 20th. Soon thereafter the Force India team called Sutil and his teammate, Di Resta, into retirement because they could not fix the problem before the end of the race and did not want to damage their cars.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportLiveRace_38-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportLiveRace-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-48" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Paul_di_Resta_overtaking_Adrian_Sutil_2013_Malaysia.jpg" class="image"><img alt="Paul di Resta overtaking Adrian Sutil in identical cars" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/74/Paul_di_Resta_overtaking_Adrian_Sutil_2013_Malaysia.jpg/220px-Paul_di_Resta_overtaking_Adrian_Sutil_2013_Malaysia.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="110" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/74/Paul_di_Resta_overtaking_Adrian_Sutil_2013_Malaysia.jpg/330px-Paul_di_Resta_overtaking_Adrian_Sutil_2013_Malaysia.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/74/Paul_di_Resta_overtaking_Adrian_Sutil_2013_Malaysia.jpg/440px-Paul_di_Resta_overtaking_Adrian_Sutil_2013_Malaysia.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2560" data-file-height="1280" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Paul_di_Resta_overtaking_Adrian_Sutil_2013_Malaysia.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>The <a href="/wiki/Force_India" title="Force India">Force India</a> cars of <a href="/wiki/Paul_di_Resta" title="Paul di Resta">Paul di Resta</a> and <a href="/wiki/Adrian_Sutil" title="Adrian Sutil">Adrian Sutil</a> were retired less than halfway through the race due to a recurring captive wheel-nut-system failure.</div></div></div>
<p>By the end of lap 25, Vettel was less than a second behind teammate Webber and could use DRS to attempt a pass for the lead. The gap to Vettel and Webber was lowered to four-tenths of a second at the start of the next lap, as Hamilton gained on them. Rocquelin told Vettel by radio on that lap to conserve his tyres in high-speed corners, because he drew too close to Weber and was affected by the aerodynamic turbulence of airflow over his teammate's car.<sup id="cite_ref-ESPNRace_39-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ESPNRace-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-BBCWebRace_40-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCWebRace-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup> Webber also slowed to preserve his tyres so he could reach the third series of pit stops, and Vettel told the Red Bull team by radio to have his teammate relinquish the lead to him because he thought he was the faster driver.<sup id="cite_ref-WebberAutoBio_46-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-WebberAutoBio-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup> On the 29th lap, Webber went faster by three-tenths of a second and pulled away from Vettel.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportRaceHughes_21-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportRaceHughes-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-ESPNRace_39-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ESPNRace-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>The third pit-stop phase began on the 30th lap. Hamliton entered the lane to switch to hard-compound tyres, and rejoined the track in fifth place. Webber and Rosberg made their stops on the next lap for hard-compound tyres, and emerged in third and fifth. Vettel led the 32nd lap; he made his stop and returned in fourth position, behind Hamilton and Webber. Button led laps 33 and 34.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportLiveRace_38-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportLiveRace-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup> Webber unsuccessfully challenged Button for first place near the final corner;<sup id="cite_ref-ESPNRace_39-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ESPNRace-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup> he then used DRS and out-braked Button to reclaim the lead before turn one of lap 35.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportLiveRace_38-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportLiveRace-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-BBCWebRace_40-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCWebRace-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup> On the 36th lap, Button had a problematic pit stop;<sup id="cite_ref-STRace_42-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-STRace-42">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup> a fault in the McLaren micro-switch pit-stop lighting system erroneously shone a green light for 120 milliseconds, and Button was released from his pit box before a mechanic could install his right-front wheel.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportRaceHughes_21-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportRaceHughes-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup> Mechanics pushed Button's car back to the pit stall for the job to be completed.<sup id="cite_ref-BBCWebRace_40-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCWebRace-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup> Button lost two minutes in the pit lane, and emerged one lap behind in 14th position.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportLiveRace_38-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportLiveRace-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup> At the front of the field, Hamilton was asked to conserve fuel when Mercedes was unable to adapt to the speed of the faster Red Bull cars; Vettel used DRS into turn one, passing Hamilton for second place on lap 39.<sup id="cite_ref-BBCWebRace_40-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCWebRace-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-F1Analysis_49-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-F1Analysis-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Vettel began to draw clear of Hamilton. On lap 41, Hülkenberg locked his tyres in the final corner and Räikkönen overtook him on the inside for eighth place at turns one and two. Hamilton began the final sequence of pit stops at the end of the lap, and was followed by Rosberg and the Red Bull duo of Webber and Vettel.<sup id="cite_ref-ESPNRace_39-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ESPNRace-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-BBCWebRace_40-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCWebRace-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup> Webber rejoined the race on an old set of hard-compound tyres,<sup id="cite_ref-WebberAutoBio_46-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-WebberAutoBio-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup> holding off his teammate Vettel through turns one to four to retain the lead.<sup id="cite_ref-BBCWebRace_40-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCWebRace-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup> Red Bull invoked <a href="/wiki/Team_orders" title="Team orders">team orders</a> on Vettel and Webber, with the code "Multi-Map 21", telling both drivers to lower engine performance and remain in first and second position (without challenging each other) to conserve their tyres.<sup id="cite_ref-F1RacingMag_2-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-F1RacingMag-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-AutosportRaceHughes_21-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportRaceHughes-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-WebberAutoBio_46-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-WebberAutoBio-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup> At the end of the lap, Rosberg used DRS to pass teammate Hamilton at the hairpin; Hamilton retook the position before turn one.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportRaceHughes_21-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportRaceHughes-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Sebastian_Vettel_overtaking_Mark_Webber_2013_Malaysia_2.jpg" class="image"><img alt="Sebastian Vettel passing teammate Mark Webber" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4c/Sebastian_Vettel_overtaking_Mark_Webber_2013_Malaysia_2.jpg/220px-Sebastian_Vettel_overtaking_Mark_Webber_2013_Malaysia_2.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="110" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4c/Sebastian_Vettel_overtaking_Mark_Webber_2013_Malaysia_2.jpg/330px-Sebastian_Vettel_overtaking_Mark_Webber_2013_Malaysia_2.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4c/Sebastian_Vettel_overtaking_Mark_Webber_2013_Malaysia_2.jpg/440px-Sebastian_Vettel_overtaking_Mark_Webber_2013_Malaysia_2.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2560" data-file-height="1280" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Sebastian_Vettel_overtaking_Mark_Webber_2013_Malaysia_2.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Sebastian Vettel ignored Red Bull team orders, passing <a href="/wiki/Mark_Webber" title="Mark Webber">Mark Webber</a> for the lead on lap 46 to win the race.</div></div></div><p>
On the 46th lap,<sup id="cite_ref-STRace_42-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-STRace-42">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup> Vettel, avenging Webber for forcing him toward the pit wall at the start of the <a href="/wiki/2012_Brazilian_Grand_Prix" title="2012 Brazilian Grand Prix">2012 Brazilian Grand Prix</a> causing him to be hit by Williams driver <a href="/wiki/Bruno_Senna" title="Bruno Senna">Bruno Senna</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-FSAusM212018_50-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FSAusM212018-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup> turned right on the first straight and used DRS and <a href="/wiki/Kinetic_energy_recovery_system" title="Kinetic energy recovery system">KERS</a>. Webber put him towards the pit-lane barrier, with their wheels almost touching at about 180&#160;mph (290&#160;km/h). Webber used the outside to keep Vettel behind at turn two, placing himself away from the <a href="/wiki/Racing_line" title="Racing line">racing line</a>, and Vettel accelerated faster out of turn three. Vettel turned left cresting a hill into turn four, overtaking Webber with better traction for the lead out of the corner.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportRaceHughes_21-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportRaceHughes-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-BBCWebRace_40-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCWebRace-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup> Red Bull team principal Christian Horner reprimanded Vettel by radio: "This is silly, Seb. Come on."<sup id="cite_ref-BBCWebRace_40-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCWebRace-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup> At the start of lap 47, Webber tried to pass Vettel into turn one; Vettel placed Webber on the edge of the track to prevent his teammate from driving onto the outside at turn two.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportRaceHughes_21-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportRaceHughes-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup> On that lap, Maldonado retired with a KERS failure.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportLiveRace_38-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportLiveRace-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-F1Analysis_49-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-F1Analysis-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup></p><div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Sergio_Perez_2013_Malaysia_FP2.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ec/Sergio_Perez_2013_Malaysia_FP2.jpg/220px-Sergio_Perez_2013_Malaysia_FP2.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="110" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ec/Sergio_Perez_2013_Malaysia_FP2.jpg/330px-Sergio_Perez_2013_Malaysia_FP2.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ec/Sergio_Perez_2013_Malaysia_FP2.jpg/440px-Sergio_Perez_2013_Malaysia_FP2.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2560" data-file-height="1280" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Sergio_Perez_2013_Malaysia_FP2.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Sergio_P%C3%A9rez" title="Sergio Pérez">Sergio Pérez</a> finished ninth, driving the race's fastest lap on the final lap.</div></div></div>
<p>Massa made a pit stop on the 47th lap to switch to medium-compound tyres when he was unable to pass Grosjean, and emerged in eighth position.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportRaceHughes_21-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportRaceHughes-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-AutosportLiveRace_38-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportLiveRace-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup> Räikkönen passed Pérez on the inside on the hairpin for sixth place on lap 49. Massa then passed Pérez on the first turn for seventh position; Pérez had used DRS to challenge Räikkönen, who was then passed by Massa for sixth.<sup id="cite_ref-ESPNRace_39-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ESPNRace-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup> Rosberg begged Mercedes team principal <a href="/wiki/Ross_Brawn" title="Ross Brawn">Ross Brawn</a> to let him pass teammate Hamilton on lap 50; Brawn refused, wanting to ensure that both cars finished the race and trying to control Hamilton's pace to improve his position in the World Drivers' Championship.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportRaceHughes_21-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportRaceHughes-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-NYTimesRace_51-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-NYTimesRace-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup> Two laps later, Ricciardo retired with a faulty exhaust system.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportLiveRace_38-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportLiveRace-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-F1Analysis_49-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-F1Analysis-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup> Massa then retook fifth from Grosjean on the straight linking the hairpin.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportLiveRace_38-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportLiveRace-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-BBCWebRace_40-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCWebRace-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup> On the 55th lap, Button retired with vibration caused by a lock in his left front <a href="/wiki/Car_suspension" title="Car suspension">suspension</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-F1Analysis_49-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-F1Analysis-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-52" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup> That lap, Pérez made a pit stop for hard-compound tyres after Hülkenberg passed him on the inside for eighth place at the fourth corner.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportLiveRace_38-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportLiveRace-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup> He retained ninth place, ahead of Vergne in tenth.<sup id="cite_ref-ESPNRace_39-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ESPNRace-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On the final lap, Brawn radioed Hamilton to conserve fuel to finish the race as Rosberg held position.<sup id="cite_ref-ESPNRace_39-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ESPNRace-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup> Vettel had his first victory of the season, his third in Malaysia (after winning in <a href="/wiki/2010_Malaysian_Grand_Prix" title="2010 Malaysian Grand Prix">2010</a> and <a href="/wiki/2011_Malaysian_Grand_Prix" title="2011 Malaysian Grand Prix">2011</a>) and the 27th of his career,<sup id="cite_ref-NYTimesRace_51-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-NYTimesRace-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup> which tied him with three-time world champion <a href="/wiki/Jackie_Stewart" title="Jackie Stewart">Jackie Stewart</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-F1RacingMag_2-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-F1RacingMag-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup> Webber finished 4.298 seconds later behind in second, and Hamilton had his first podium finish with Mercedes in third.<sup id="cite_ref-ESPNRace_39-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ESPNRace-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup> Rosberg and Massa were fourth and fifth, and Grosjean and Räikkönen were sixth and seventh. Hülkenberg took eighth, Sauber's first points of the season.<sup id="cite_ref-BBCWebRace_40-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCWebRace-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup> Pérez took ninth, and set the race's <a href="/wiki/Fastest_lap" title="Fastest lap">fastest lap</a> on the final lap: 1 minute, 39.199 seconds. Vergne was tenth, and the final finishers were Bottas, Gutiérrez, Bianchi, Pic, Van Der Garde, Chilton, Button and Ricciardo.<sup id="cite_ref-F1RacingMag_2-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-F1RacingMag-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup> After the race, Webber cut across Vettel in anger over how his teammate won.<sup id="cite_ref-53" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-53">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Post-race">Post-race</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2013_Malaysian_Grand_Prix&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: Post-race">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Lewis_Hamilton_2013_Malaysia_FP2_1.jpg" class="image"><img alt="Lewis Hamilton during a practice session" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fe/Lewis_Hamilton_2013_Malaysia_FP2_1.jpg/220px-Lewis_Hamilton_2013_Malaysia_FP2_1.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="110" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fe/Lewis_Hamilton_2013_Malaysia_FP2_1.jpg/330px-Lewis_Hamilton_2013_Malaysia_FP2_1.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fe/Lewis_Hamilton_2013_Malaysia_FP2_1.jpg/440px-Lewis_Hamilton_2013_Malaysia_FP2_1.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2560" data-file-height="1280" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Lewis_Hamilton_2013_Malaysia_FP2_1.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Lewis_Hamilton" title="Lewis Hamilton">Lewis Hamilton</a> had his first podium finish with the <a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_in_Formula_One" title="Mercedes-Benz in Formula One">Mercedes</a> team.</div></div></div>
<p>Red Bull technical director <a href="/wiki/Adrian_Newey" title="Adrian Newey">Adrian Newey</a> told Webber that Vettel was instructed to hold position.<sup id="cite_ref-WebberAutoBio_46-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-WebberAutoBio-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup> Incensed about Vettel's action, Webber considered boycotting the podium ceremony until convinced to do otherwise.<sup id="cite_ref-RBRow_54-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-RBRow-54">&#91;54&#93;</a></sup> In the cool-down room, Vettel wanted to speak to Webber, who did not want to communicate with him;<sup id="cite_ref-WebberAutoBio_46-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-WebberAutoBio-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup> he sat on a chair and told Vettel, "Multi 21, Seb. Multi 21".<sup id="cite_ref-BBCWebRace_40-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCWebRace-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup> During the podium interviews by pundit and former driver <a href="/wiki/Martin_Brundle" title="Martin Brundle">Martin Brundle</a>, Vettel said that it was "very close wheel-to-wheel racing" with Webber.<sup id="cite_ref-PressConf_55-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PressConf-55">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup> Webber said that Vettel made an independent decision to pass him, and Red Bull would protect him.<sup id="cite_ref-PressConf_55-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PressConf-55">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup> Hamilton said that his teammate, Rosberg, should have finished third because the latter was faster.<sup id="cite_ref-PressConf_55-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PressConf-55">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup> During the post-race press conference, Vettel called himself "the <a href="/wiki/Black_sheep" title="Black sheep">black sheep</a>" for prioritising himself over the Red Bull team.<sup id="cite_ref-PressConf_55-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PressConf-55">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup> Webber said in the final 15 laps, he "was thinking that many things, yes. Many many things" about previous races and the current one.<sup id="cite_ref-PressConf_55-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PressConf-55">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup> Hamilton said that he would ask Mercedes if he could apologise to his teammate, Rosberg.<sup id="cite_ref-PressConf_55-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PressConf-55">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Mark_Webber_2013_Malaysia_FP1.jpg" class="image"><img alt="Mark Webber at a practice session" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ad/Mark_Webber_2013_Malaysia_FP1.jpg/220px-Mark_Webber_2013_Malaysia_FP1.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="110" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ad/Mark_Webber_2013_Malaysia_FP1.jpg/330px-Mark_Webber_2013_Malaysia_FP1.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ad/Mark_Webber_2013_Malaysia_FP1.jpg/440px-Mark_Webber_2013_Malaysia_FP1.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2560" data-file-height="1280" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Mark_Webber_2013_Malaysia_FP1.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Mark Webber was asked by Red Bull founder and co-owner Dietrich Mateschitz to give an oral and written account of Vettel's actions.</div></div></div>
<p>Vettel ignoring team orders was a key moment in his rivalry with Webber, which began when he collided with Webber at the <a href="/wiki/2010_Turkish_Grand_Prix" title="2010 Turkish Grand Prix">2010 Turkish Grand Prix</a> and was forced to retire.<sup id="cite_ref-56" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-56">&#91;56&#93;</a></sup> Horner talked to Vettel and Webber the night after the race, expressing his misgivings about the situation.<sup id="cite_ref-RBRow_54-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-RBRow-54">&#91;54&#93;</a></sup> Vettel flew from Kuala Lumpur to visit the Red Bull team factory in <a href="/wiki/Milton_Keynes" title="Milton Keynes">Milton Keynes</a>, England on 26 March to apologise to his colleagues after doing so to Webber at the press conference. According to Horner, Vettel was eager to make up for the wrongdoing and shook hands with Webber: "He can't turn back the clock, but he's accepted what he did was wrong."<sup id="cite_ref-57" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-57">&#91;57&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-58" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-58">&#91;58&#93;</a></sup> Red Bull did not reprimand or punish Vettel because his lawyers threatened legal action; he told Webber at the <a href="/wiki/2013_Chinese_Grand_Prix" title="2013 Chinese Grand Prix">Chinese Grand Prix</a> three weeks later that he was annoyed by his teammate's comments on the podium.<sup id="cite_ref-WebberAutoBio_46-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-WebberAutoBio-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup> Vettel later recanted his apology for winning: "Obviously I realised at that moment there was quite a conflict. On the one hand I am the kind of guy who respects team decisions and on the other hand, probably Mark is not the one who deserved it (to win) at the time. The bottom line is I was racing, I was faster, I passed him, I won."<sup id="cite_ref-59" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-59">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Webber received a telephone call in Australia from Red Bull owner and co-founder <a href="/wiki/Dietrich_Mateschitz" title="Dietrich Mateschitz">Dietrich Mateschitz</a>, who asked him to provide an oral and written account of events because he was irate about the damage to his company's reputation.<sup id="cite_ref-WebberAutoBio_46-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-WebberAutoBio-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup> Although media reports and comments from the Formula One community speculated about his future at Red Bull and whether reserve driver, <a href="/wiki/S%C3%A9bastien_Buemi" title="Sébastien Buemi">Sébastien Buemi</a>, would replace him,<sup id="cite_ref-60" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-60">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup> Webber dismissed the suggestions and would continue driving for the team for the foreseeable future and talk to Mateschitz about his future later in the year.<sup id="cite_ref-61" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-61">&#91;61&#93;</a></sup> Webber said seven years later he believes Vettel may regret the incident, but added that he was not " an angel at certain other events here and there."<sup id="cite_ref-62" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-62">&#91;62&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Jenson_Button_2013_Malaysia_FP2_2.jpg" class="image"><img alt="Jenson Button during a practice session" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/eb/Jenson_Button_2013_Malaysia_FP2_2.jpg/220px-Jenson_Button_2013_Malaysia_FP2_2.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="110" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/eb/Jenson_Button_2013_Malaysia_FP2_2.jpg/330px-Jenson_Button_2013_Malaysia_FP2_2.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/eb/Jenson_Button_2013_Malaysia_FP2_2.jpg/440px-Jenson_Button_2013_Malaysia_FP2_2.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2560" data-file-height="1280" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Jenson_Button_2013_Malaysia_FP2_2.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Jenson_Button" title="Jenson Button">Jenson Button</a> retired with three laps to go with a vibration caused by a lock of his <a href="/wiki/McLaren" title="McLaren">McLaren</a>'s left front <a href="/wiki/Car_suspension" title="Car suspension">suspension</a>.</div></div></div>
<p>Alonso said that he could have challenged for the victory had he not retired on the second lap due to Ferrari's similar race pace to Red Bull: "No one was especially quick, so I think we could really have fought for the win."<sup id="cite_ref-63" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-63">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup> According to Button, he could have battled Mercedes for third position on strategy.<sup id="cite_ref-64" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-64">&#91;64&#93;</a></sup> Although Rosberg begged Ross Brawn to reconsider his decision to maintain position, he respected Mercedes' judgment and finishing third and fourth and duelling Red Bull was "such a milestone".<sup id="cite_ref-65" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-65">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup> Mercedes motorsport boss <a href="/wiki/Toto_Wolff" title="Toto Wolff">Toto Wolff</a> said about Rosberg was unhappy about the situation but understood the decision to hold position: "We are all grown ups and they are grown up. They are professional sportsmen and they understand that sometimes there can be a certain controversy in a certain situation."<sup id="cite_ref-66" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-66">&#91;66&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>The result moved Vettel into the lead of the World Drivers' Championship with 40 points, and Räikkönen fell to second place. Webber rose three positions to third place, Hamilton moved to fourth, and Massa dropped from fourth to fifth place.<sup id="cite_ref-2013Points_6-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2013Points-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup> Red Bull took the lead of the World Constructors' Championship with 60 points. Lotus maintained second place, and Ferrari fell from first to third. Mercedes and Force India retained fourth and fifth place, with 17 races left in the season.<sup id="cite_ref-2013Points_6-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2013Points-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Race_classification">Race classification</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2013_Malaysian_Grand_Prix&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: Race classification">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Drivers who scored <a href="/wiki/List_of_Formula_One_World_Championship_points_scoring_systems" title="List of Formula One World Championship points scoring systems">championship points</a> are denoted in <b>bold</b>.
</p>
